<Review>This place is crowded almost all the time, but you can't blame them as they have some of the lowest gas prices in the city.

You have the option of paying for a car wash at the pump (and coming back another day for the wash, if the line is too long). I believe the code is good for at least a week, if not 30 days (I don't remember).

The store is clean and well-lit. Since the store is bigger than most in Carson, they have a little more variety in products. I've found the associates to be helpful and courteous.<//Review>< pictures>

<Text>Pretty nice station as it is well lit, well stocked, and fuel prices are cheaper than most. Sometimes the card readers at the pump don't work properly. The restroom toilet is stained with feces frequently lately. My main issue is that most of the staff are unfriendly. I went the other night to purchase fuel and a lotto ticket using my debit card and the young lady had no issue.

The following evening, I go again for the same thing and purchase the exact same way, and the male cashier scolds me for not telling him beforehand that I was purchasing a lotto ticket using my debit card. He went ahead and performed the function but he pushed my receipt and ticket at me like some little kid. The staff weren't unfriendly similar to this when the place was new. The female cashiers are generally a little better but the male ones are very unfriendly.

I am tired of coming here and frequently experiencing the poor attitude of the staff. Only 2-3 of them are nice. I only come now when it is convenient for me and I try to now avoid going in. They're probably tired of seeing me too, so I have remedied that by making the extra drive to Sepulveda Blvd. and visit the ARCO and Chevron down there. At least they're friendlier.< /Text><pics>None<//pics>< Response>

< text>
Amazing caverns in the Mojave desert. The tours are not running right now due to Covid. When they are running it is hard to get into one. They only run Friday, Saturday, Sunday twice a day, 15 people only. Book early and really try to see them!< /text>
<pics>None</pics><Resp>None< /Resp><Gmap_id>0x80cf8e5a63200a35:0xe0903b2baf1beb97<//Gmap_id></record></dataset><record>
< Review>
A little known, hidden gem in the middle of nowhere, this 2 hour tour is very much worth with the visit. Our tour guide, Will, is personable and humorous. The pathway to the cavern was just recently built or renovated within a year or so. This place was privately owned and hand-built by a couple who later passed away in the 1980‚Äôs then sold off to the State Parks. Lots of cool facts about this place that I‚Äôd consider still part of recent history.

Pricing: $10 adult, $5 children and $10 parking.

Fun facts I learned: this limestone cavern is so solid it withstand earthquakes. A great hideout place in natural disaster.

This place deserves more attention and protection. Really worth the drive to pay a visit. A nice walk through living history.</Review>

<username>sharry hope< /username><date>1546190822709< /date>< Rate>
4< /Rate>
<text>Dinosaur Hill Park has been here since I can remember. (1955) It is right in back of the house my Dad built at that time on Random Way. I loved climbing the hill up to the top so I could see the incredible view!!!  I went there December  28th 2018 for the first time since 1960. WOW!!! The day was so clear and the view was just spectacular!!! I took some pictures that I added the photos to this place on Google maps.
The only reasons I didn't give dinosaur Hill Park five stars is because there are no facilities here and it really needs some work for access especially for the handicapped. There is just a dirt path and there are some rickety stairs not to be trusted. This area is not really accessible during the rain or when it's really wet. There is no pavement and and no cement. Just dirt and mud and grass. There is a handicap parking place and the pathway is accessible if it is dry. Another thing I was disappointed in was that people have spray-painted graffiti on the interesting natural rocks and boulders.
Please be respectful of this place<//text>< Pics>

< user_id>
106553283737605907854< /user_id>
<name>Katie Bunny</name>< date>
1473175863264<//date>
< rating>
4<//rating>
< review>
Parking area is very small, fitting up to 5 to 7 cars with 1 handicap spot. The view from the parking lot isn't the best one out there, but it's something.
Once you hike up the hill to the top you can see some great views overlooking contra costa county and Mount Diablo. I love to fly kites here on windy days or on relax in the sun on the warm and sunny days.
A lot of teenagers and the under 25 crowd like to congregate here, especially during the afternoon, evening, and throughout the night. Some of them are only looking for a place to smoke weed etc. Very few are looking for trouble.
But it's never been an issue for me, more of just an observation. Most of the time they are just chillin like you are and have no quams. There's always a bad egg amount the bunch, so don't let that deter you from coming here.<//review>

<name>Joby George< /name><Date>1618529524308< /Date><Rating>4</Rating>< Text>
Visit Visa experience:

I have applied for a Visit Visa with San Jose Mexican Consulate General and the over all experience was very good. The security was very strict with the appointment time and the staff inside was very good and we came out with visa in 45 mins! Just paid $44 for the visa and all the supporting documents (application form, photo, bank statements etc) and a short interview by the officer. They took another photo inside, finger prints and printed the visa and provided the stamped passport immediately. I found very professional for the visa service.

Now the only downside is getting an appointment for consulate interview! It always shows no appointment and there is no way we can connect to them using the phone as it always go to voicemail. Luckily I found their Facebook page and chatted on the messenger and the operator told me they release the appointments on Tuesday afternoon. I checked on that website (MEXITEL) everyday 5-6 times and one Tuesday afternoon I got two appointments for me and my wife and it quickly gets filled in few minutes !<//Text>
